The_DT Clear_NNP Skies_NNPS Act_NNP

The_DT Clear_NNP Skies_NNPS Act_NNP would_MD reduce_VB emissions_NNS of_IN sulfur_NN dioxide_NN
(_( SO_NNP 2_LS )_) ,_, nitrogen_NN oxides_NNS (_( NOx_NNP )_) ,_, and_CC mercury_NN from_IN fossil_JJ fuel-fired_JJ
combustion_NN units_NNS by_IN approximately_RB 70_CD %_NN from_IN current_JJ levels_NNS ._. 1_LS These_DT
mandatory_JJ emission_NN reductions_NNS would_MD be_VB achieved_VBN through_IN a_DT cap_NN and_CC
trade_NN
1_LS The_DT Clear_NNP Skies_NNPS Act_NNP would_MD cut_VB sulfur_NN dioxide_NN (_( SO_NNP 2_LS )_) emissions_NNS
by_IN 73_CD percent_NN ,_, from_IN current_JJ emissions_NNS of_IN 11_CD million_CD tons_NNS to_TO caps_NNS of_IN
4_CD ._. 5_CD million_CD tons_NNS in_IN 2010_CD and_CC 3_CD million_CD tons_NNS in_IN 2018_CD ._. It_PRP would_MD cut_VB
emissions_NNS of_IN nitrogen_NN oxides_NNS (_( NOx_NNP )_) by_IN 67_CD percent_NN ,_, from_IN current_JJ
emissions_NNS of_IN 5_CD million_CD tons_NNS
program_NN ,_, modeled_VBD on_IN the_DT current_JJ Acid_NNP Rain_NN Program_NN for_IN SO_NNP 2_CD ._.
Federally_NNP enforceable_JJ emissions_NNS limits_NNS ,_, or_CC national_JJ caps_NNS ,_, for_IN each_DT
pollutant_NN would_MD be_VB established_VBN ._. Sources_NNS would_MD be_VB allowed_VBN to_TO

remaining_VBG environmental_JJ and_CC health_NN problems_NNS associated_VBN with_IN power_NN

Exhibit_NN 2_CD outlines_VBZ the_DT analytical_JJ framework_NN used_VBN to_TO study_VB the_DT
benefits_NNS of_IN the_DT Clear_NNP Skies_NNPS Act_NNP ._. The_DT first_JJ step_NN in_IN the_DT benefits_NNS

proposed_VBN regulation_NN and_CC one_CD or_CC more_JJR control_NN scenarios_NNS that_WDT simulate_VBP
conditions_NNS under_IN the_DT regulations_NNS being_VBG evaluated_VBN ._. The_DT benefits_NNS of_IN a_DT

IPM_NNP is_VBZ a_DT linear_JJ programming_NN model_NN of_IN the_DT electricity_NN sector_NN that_WDT

(_( i_NNP ._. e_SYM ._. least_JJS cost_NN )_) approach_NN to_TO operating_VBG the_DT electric_JJ power_NN

(_( e_SYM ._. g_SYM ._. pollution_NN caps_NNS or_CC transmission_NN limitations_NNS )_) ._. The_DT model_NN ,_, which_WDT
was_VBD developed_VBN for_IN EPA_NNP by_IN ICF_NNP Resources_NNPS ,_, Inc_NNP ._. ,_, selects_VBZ investment_NN
strategies_NNS given_VBN the_DT cost_NN and_CC performance_NN characteristics_NNS of_IN
available_JJ options_NNS ,_, forecasts_NNS of_IN customer_NN demand_NN for_IN electricity_NN ,_,
and_CC reliability_NN criteria_NNS ._. System_NNP dispatch_VB ,_, which_WDT determines_VBZ the_DT
proper_JJ and_CC most_RBS efficient_JJ use_NN of_IN the_DT existing_VBG and_CC new_JJ resources_NNS
available_JJ to_TO utilities_NNS and_CC their_PRP$ customers_NNS ,_, is_VBZ optimized_JJ given_VBN the_DT
resource_NN mix_NN ,_, unit_NN operating_NN characteristics_NNS ,_, and_CC fuel_NN and_CC other_JJ
costs_NNS ._. Unit_NNP and_CC system_NN operating_NN constraints_NNS provide_VBP

The_DT IPM_NNP is_VBZ dynamic_JJ ;_: it_PRP has_VBZ the_DT capability_NN to_TO use_VB forecasts_NNS of_IN

athttp_NN :_: /_NN /_NN www_NN ._. epa_NN ._. gov_NN /_NN airmarkt_NN /_NN epa-ipm_JJ /_NN index_NN ._. html_NN #_# documentation_NN

estimating_VBG PM_NNP concentrations_NNS ._. Atmospheric_NNP transformation_NN of_IN

Regional_NNP Modeling_NNP System_NNP for_IN Aerosols_NNP and_CC Deposition_NNP
(_( REMSAD_NNP )_)
The_DT change_NN in_IN PM_NNP concentrations_NNS due_JJ to_TO the_DT Clear_NNP Skies_NNPS Act_NNP was_VBD
modeled_VBN using_VBG the_DT Regional_NNP Modeling_NNP System_NNP for_IN Aerosols_NNP and_CC
Deposition_NNP (_( REMSAD_NNP )_) ._. REMSAD_NNP was_VBD also_RB used_VBN to_TO estimate_VB the_DT changes_NNS
in_IN visibility_NN and_CC deposition_NN of_IN mercury_NN ,_, nitrogen_NN ,_, and_CC sulfur_NN ._.
REMSAD_NNP is_VBZ a_DT three-dimensional_JJ ,_, grid-based_JJ Eulerian_NNP air_NN quality_NN
model_NN designed_VBN to_TO simulate_VBP long-term_JJ (_( e_SYM ._. g_SYM ._. ,_, annual_JJ )_) concentrations_NNS
and_CC deposition_NN fluxes_NNS of_IN atmospheric_JJ pollutants_NNS over_IN large_JJ spatial_NN
scales_NNS (_( e_SYM ._. g_SYM ._. ,_, over_IN the_DT contiguous_JJ U_NNP ._. S_NNP ._. )_) ._. Air_NN pollution_NN issues_NNS meant_VBN
to_TO be_VB addressed_VBN by_IN REMSAD_NNP include_VBP long-term_JJ PM_NNP 2_CD ._. 5_LS ambient_NN
concentrations_NNS ;_: visibility_NN ;_: ambient_NN concentrations_NNS and_CC deposition_NN
fluxes_NNS of_IN several_JJ hazardous_JJ air_NN pollutants_NNS ,_, including_VBG mercury_NN ;_:
deposition_NN fluxes_NNS of_IN nutrient_NN nitrogen_NN ;_: and_CC deposition_NN of_IN acids_NNS
such_JJ as_IN sulfuric_JJ acid_NN and_CC nitric_JJ acid_NN ._.
REMSAD_NNP has_VBZ been_VBN developed_VBN under_IN funding_NN from_IN the_DT U_NNP ._. S_NNP ._.
Environmental_NNP Protection_NNP Agency_NNP over_IN the_DT past_JJ five_CD years_NNS ._. REMSAD_NNP

To_TO estimate_VB health_NN benefits_NNS from_IN the_DT Clear_NNP Skies_NNPS Act_NNP ,_, we_PRP used_VBD
the_DT same_JJ general_JJ approach_NN used_VBN in_IN recent_JJ major_JJ OAR_NNP regulatory_JJ
analyses_NNS (_( U_NNP ._. S_NNP ._. EPA_NNP ,_, 1999_CD a_DT ,_, 1999_CD b_SYM and_CC 2000_CD b_SYM )_) ._. This_DT approach_NN takes_VBZ

contiguous_JJ

Study_NN population_NN

(_( e_SYM ._. g_SYM ._. ,_, asthmatics_NNS ,_, children_NNS ,_, elderly_JJ )_) ._. However_RB ,_, there_EX are_VBP tradeoffs_NNS
to_TO comprehensiveness_NN of_IN study_NN population_NN ._. Selecting_NNP a_DT C-R_NNP function_NN
from_IN a_DT study_NN that_WDT considered_VBD all_DT ages_NNS will_MD avoid_VB omitting_VBG the_DT
benefits_NNS associated_VBN with_IN any_DT population_NN age_NN category_NN ._. However_RB ,_, if_IN
the_DT age_NN distribution_NN of_IN a_DT study_NN population_NN from_IN an_DT "_'' all_DT population_NN "_''

population_NN ,_, and_CC if_IN pollutant_NN effects_NNS vary_VBP by_IN age_NN ,_, then_RB bias_NN can_MD be_VB
introduced_VBN into_IN the_DT benefits_NNS analysis_NN ._.
Study_NN location_NN U_NNP ._. S_NNP ._. studies_NNS are_VBP more_RBR desirable_JJ than_IN non-_NN U_NNP ._. S_NNP ._.
studies_NNS because_IN of_IN potential_JJ differences_NNS in_IN pollution_NN
characteristics_NNS ,_, exposure_NN patterns_NNS ,_, medical_JJ care_NN system_NN ,_, and_CC life_NN

Pollutants_NNP included_VBN in_IN model_NN Models_NNP with_IN more_JJR pollutants_NNS are_VBP
generally_RB preferred_VBN to_TO models_NNS with_IN fewer_JJR pollutants_NNS ,_, though_IN careful_JJ
attention_NN must_MD be_VB paid_VBN to_TO potential_JJ colinearity_NN between_IN pollutants_NNS ._.
Because_IN PM_NNP has_VBZ been_VBN acknowledged_VBN to_TO be_VB an_DT important_JJ and_CC pervasive_JJ
pollutant_NN ,_, models_NNS that_WDT include_VBP some_DT measure_NN of_IN PM_NNP are_VBP highly_RB
preferred_VBN to_TO those_DT that_WDT do_VBP not_RB ._.
Measure_NN of_IN PM_NNP PM_NNP 2_CD ._. 5_LS and_CC PM_NNP 10_CD are_VBP preferred_VBN to_TO other_JJ measures_NNS of_IN
particulate_NN matter_NN ,_, such_JJ as_IN total_JJ suspended_VBN particulate_NN matter_NN
